# RenderMan 27 Codex Translation Progress

## Policy

- Translation is authored by Codex. Work may be grouped into small batches for throughput, but every source HTML page is still translated, applied, and audited as its own countable unit.
- No external machine translation service is used.
- Scripts only extract text nodes, apply Codex-authored JSONL translations, preserve HTML structure, and validate layout/terminology.
- The active glossary is `glossary/renderman_terminology.json`.
- After each audited small stage is marked done, report total progress as completed source HTML pages / total source HTML pages / percentage. Page-internal sub-stages must still report the unchanged page total until the whole source page passes the full audit. Only pages that have passed layout, glossary, tag, source-residual, ASCII-heavy, and placement audits count as completed.
- To improve speed, upcoming small stages use dynamic text-volume batching: low-risk short pages may be grouped into larger batches when the total source text stays manageable, while each page still keeps per-page JSONL, precheck, apply report, independent audit, and readability review. Long or terminology-dense pages remain single-page stages.
- Throughput adjustment after user feedback on speed: before each resumed run, build the next batch from actual source text-node counts and reuse already audited identical source text from the translation cache where applicable. This keeps the Codex-authored requirement intact while reducing repeated manual work and per-page bookkeeping overhead.

## Progress Accounting

- Total source HTML pages: 816.
- Completed audited unique source pages: 816.
- Current completion: 816 / 816 = 100.00%.
- Last updated: 2026-06-26 12:03:12 CST; final all-source/all-target consistency audit passed after Phase 823.
- Active Phase: none. All 816 unique source HTML pages have been translated, applied, independently audited, counted, and final-audited.
- Current execution preference: complete. Future work should be limited to review, polish, packaging, or handling newly added source pages.
- Accounting correction: the completed-phase table contains 818 `done` rows, but two historical rows duplicate the same source paths (`REN27/542236544-txmake.html` and `REN27/542236770-Custom OCIO Config.html`). Current and future percentages use de-duplicated source HTML paths, so the authoritative unique-page count after Phase 823 is 816 / 816.
